<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-q31-what-is-faster-loc-or-at" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#q31-what-is-faster-loc-or-at"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Q31: what is faster, <code>loc</code>, or <code>at</code>?</h3>
<p dir="auto">Answer with a line plot, similar to the one for the previous question.  Here is a code snippet to use for the measurement (adapt to measure <code>.at</code> as well):</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# HOW LONG DOES THIS TAKE TO RUN, FOR DATAFRAMES WITH DIFFERENT NUMBERS OF ROWS?
total = 0
for idx in df.index:
    for col in df.columns:
        total += df.loc[idx, col]"><pre><span class="pl-c"># HOW LONG DOES THIS TAKE TO RUN, FOR DATAFRAMES WITH DIFFERENT NUMBERS OF ROWS?</span>
<span class="pl-s1">total</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">idx</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">df</span>.<span class="pl-s1">index</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">col</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">df</span>.<span class="pl-s1">columns</span>:
        <span class="pl-s1">total</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">df</span>.<span class="pl-s1">loc</span>[<span class="pl-s1">idx</span>, <span class="pl-s1">col</span>]</pre></div>
<h3 tabindex="-1" dir="auto"><a id="user-content-q32-what-is-faster-a-loop-or-apply" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" tabindex="-1" href="#q32-what-is-faster-a-loop-or-apply"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a>Q32: what is faster, a loop or <code>.apply</code>?</h3>
<p dir="auto">Answer this one with a line plot similar as to the last two.  You should, however, have measurements going up to 20000 rows.</p>
<p dir="auto">For the two code snippets to measure:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# HOW LONG DOES THIS TAKE TO RUN, FOR DATAFRAMES WITH DIFFERENT NUMBERS OF ROWS?
result = df[&quot;A&quot;].apply(laugh).tolist()"><pre><span class="pl-c"># HOW LONG DOES THIS TAKE TO RUN, FOR DATAFRAMES WITH DIFFERENT NUMBERS OF ROWS?</span>
<span class="pl-s1">result</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-s1">df</span>[<span class="pl-s">"A"</span>].<span class="pl-en">apply</span>(<span class="pl-s1">laugh</span>).<span class="pl-en">tolist</span>()</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">AND</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="# HOW LONG DOES THIS TAKE TO RUN, FOR DATAFRAMES WITH DIFFERENT NUMBERS OF ROWS?
result = []
for val in df[&quot;A&quot;]:
    result.append(laugh(val))"><pre><span class="pl-c"># HOW LONG DOES THIS TAKE TO RUN, FOR DATAFRAMES WITH DIFFERENT NUMBERS OF ROWS?</span>
<span class="pl-s1">result</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> []
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s1">val</span> <span class="pl-c1">in</span> <span class="pl-s1">df</span>[<span class="pl-s">"A"</span>]:
    <span class="pl-s1">result</span>.<span class="pl-en">append</span>(<span class="pl-en">laugh</span>(<span class="pl-s1">val</span>))</pre></div>
<p dir="auto">The <code>laugh</code> function is defined as follows:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="def laugh(x):
    return &quot;ha&quot; * x"><pre><span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">laugh</span>(<span class="pl-s1">x</span>):
    <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-s">"ha"</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-s1">x</span></pre></div>
</article></div><button hidden=""></button></section></div></div><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 ktQnIo"></div><div class="Box-sc-g0xbh4-0 cHyvOJ panel-content-narrow-styles
